# LAYER v2026-06-25T — CASE VERIFICATION: STRICT SOURCE PASS 2

Mode: no encyclopedia, no rumor-as-fact, no comment-section evidence. Publish only what can be phrased proportionally to a stable source.

## Triage after this pass

### PUBLIC CORE — usable in article body if phrased tightly

1. Robert Morris — PUBLIC A
   - Use category: criminal child sexual abuse; judicial/criminal fact after guilty plea.
   - Safe wording: pleaded guilty to criminal counts involving lewd/indecent acts with a child; sex-offender registration / sentence / restitution only as reported by court-news sources.
   - Do NOT write: moral failure, inappropriate relationship, affair, young lady.
   - Pattern: language minimization is itself part of the moral lesson.

2. SBC / Guidepost — PUBLIC A-/B+
   - Use category: systemic institutional failure around abuse reports.
   - Safe wording: Guidepost investigation commissioned by SBC Executive Committee found long patterns of resistance, stonewalling, hostility toward survivors, and liability-protective information control.
   - Pattern: systems can use polity, liability and procedural language to avoid protecting the weak.

3. RZIM / Ravi Zacharias — PUBLIC A-/B+ only when tied to the independent investigation/reporting trail
   - Use category: platform predator / ministry-enabled concealment / donor-trust collapse.
   - Safe wording: independent investigation found credible evidence of sexual misconduct; use investigative report and major reporting, not summaries.
   - Need to preserve exact report title/source and avoid secondary inflation.

4. Willow Creek / Bill Hybels — PUBLIC B+ pending direct PDF/report capture
   - Use category: celebrity-founder protection, mishandled allegations, independent review credibility finding.
   - Safe wording: independent advisory review found allegations credible; do not add details unless direct report or major reporting supports them.

### LIMITED — usable only as narrow typological examples, not core proof

5. Art Azurdia — LIMITED
   - Safe narrow thesis: a preacher may have truly helped hearers while hiding sin; God’s work through a sermon does not justify the preacher or preserve qualification.
   - Fully safe facts: his own confession admits adulterous relationships, hidden sin, self-disqualification from elder office, and no desire to pursue ministry.
   - Trinity removal can be used only through near-primary transcript/reporting; abuse-language must be attributed to Katie Roberts and not stated as court/institutional finding unless independently confirmed.

6. Josh Buice — LIMITED
   - Safe narrow thesis: anonymous/fake-account slander and delayed confession after evidence; use only if tied to PMBC/G3 statements quoted in reliable reporting.
   - Do not use for broad abuse-of-office claims unless primary statements are captured.

7. Mark Driscoll — LIMITED B
   - Safe narrow thesis: domineering/disqualifying leadership pattern in a doctrinally conservative setting.
   - Do NOT classify as sexual/criminal/heresy case.
   - Need archived Acts 29 statement or stable major-reporting link before article-body use.

### HOLD — do not use in public article yet

8. Darrin Patrick — HOLD
   - Strong leads exist around removal for pastoral misconduct / historical pattern of sin, but direct church primary statement still not captured.
   - Do not use in final article until primary statement/archived letter is preserved.

9. Perry Noble — HOLD
   - Secondary reporting gives alcohol/family-neglect removal and later platform return; direct NewSpring statement not captured.
   - Do not use as article proof yet.

10. Tullian Tchividjian — HOLD for core article
   - Need direct PCA presbytery/deposition source or stable primary record.
   - Can be studied internally as restoration-speed/platform-return case only.

11. James MacDonald — HOLD for core article
   - Need primary Harvest/elder/independent documentation before public article use.

12. Steve Lawson — HOLD
   - Too recent / insufficiently source-closed for this package’s current standard.

## New editorial rule

A case is not “verified” because the story is widely known. It becomes usable only when the exact sentence we want to print can be proved from a stable source.

Article-safe language must be event-based:
- confessed / admitted / pleaded guilty / resigned / was removed / was deposed / independent report found / church statement said.

Avoid soul-reading:
- “repented,” “did not repent,” “was fake,” “was sincere” — unless framed as diagnostic tension from observable facts, not omniscient judgment.

## Gold synthesis

The strongest article will not be a catalogue of scandals. It should be a map of recurring patterns:

- criminal abuse renamed as moral failure;
- institutional self-protection renamed as polity;
- reputation management renamed as repentance;
- platform return renamed as restoration;
- silence renamed as unity;
- partial confession renamed as full accountability.

## Current public-core recommendation

Use only 4–6 named cases in the public series:

1. Robert Morris — naming evil without euphemism.
2. SBC/Guidepost — system failure, polity/liability as shield.
3. RZIM — platform charisma, donor trust, concealed predation.
4. Willow/Hybels — celebrity-founder culture and mishandled allegations.
5. Optional LIMITED: Azurdia — “God may bless hearers through compromised preaching, but fruit in hearers does not justify hidden sin or restore qualification.”
6. Optional LIMITED: Buice — anonymous attack / delayed confession / reputational damage control.

Everything else remains internal scaffolding until primary-source closed.

## UPDATE v2026-06-25U — строгая верификация кейсов: MacDonald / Lawson / Patrick / Perry Noble

Дата: 2026-06-25.
Метод: только source-first. Энциклопедии не использованы как доказательство; поисковые выдачи с энциклопедиями учитывались только как мусорные leads и не повышают статус кейса.

### 1. James MacDonald / Harvest Bible Chapel — STATUS: PUBLIC B+ / NEAR-PRIMARY STRONG

**Что теперь можно печатать публично:**
- James MacDonald был fired/removed Harvest Bible Chapel in February 2019.
- Christianity Today цитирует Harvest elders: removal was for conduct “contrary and harmful to the best interests of the church”; timeline accelerated after highly inappropriate recorded comments were given to media.
- Later Harvest elders said MacDonald was “biblically disqualified” from ministry, failed elder qualifications, and showed patterns including disruptive behavior, insulting/belittling/verbal bullying, improper use of positional/spiritual authority, and extravagant spending using church resources for personal benefit.
- Harvest elders wrote that fruits of repentance had not yet been evident and called for extended time away from ministry, repentance, reconciliation and restitution.

**Источники:**
- Christianity Today, “James MacDonald Fired from Harvest,” 2019-02-13. URL: https://www.christianitytoday.com/2019/02/james-macdonald-fired-harvest-bible-chapel/
- Christianity Today, “Harvest Elders Say James MacDonald Is ‘Biblically Disqualified’ From Ministry,” 2019-11-05. URL: https://www.christianitytoday.com/2019/11/harvest-elders-say-james-macdonald-biblically-disqualified/

**Классификация:**
- domineering / verbally bullying leadership;
- improper positional and spiritual authority;
- financial/stewardship concerns;
- public rebuke / extended absence / fruits-of-repentance test.

**Нельзя утверждать без отдельной первички:**
- criminal allegations as established fact;
- every financial allegation as proven;
- “false teacher” or “heretic.”

**Смысловая ценность:**
Кейс особенно силён для тезиса: disqualification is not only sexual scandal. A leader can become biblically disqualified by patterns of domineering authority, verbal bullying, misuse of spiritual authority, and lack of evident fruits of repentance.

### 2. Steven J. Lawson — STATUS: LIMITED B / MODERN REPORTING + PUBLIC APOLOGY

**Что можно аккуратно использовать:**
- Trinity Bible Church of Dallas announced in September 2024 that Lawson was no longer ministering there after admitting an inappropriate relationship.
- Chron reports that after months of silence Lawson publicly said he had sinned grievously, describing a sinful relationship with a woman not his wife and admitting betrayal/deception toward wife, children and ministries.
- Chron also reports he was removed/resigned from associated ministry roles and that content was removed by ministries.

**Источники:**
- Chron, “Former Dallas pastor breaks silence after being fired for relationship with younger woman,” 2025-03-14. URL: https://www.chron.com/culture/religion/article/texas-pastor-affair-x-fired-20220162.php

**Классификация:**
- hidden sexual sin / ministry platform;
- public apology after delayed silence;
- disqualification/restoration timing question.

**Почему не PUBLIC A:**
- пока нет сохранённого official Trinity full statement в пакете;
- не используем неподтверждённые детали про возраст/identity женщины без надёжного source chain;
- социальные сети/удалённые страницы требуют архивной проверки.

**Смысловая ценность:**
Кейс полезен не для сенсации, а для темы: сильная доктрина и строгая публичная моральная проповедь не защищают от скрытого греха; публичная ортодоксия не отменяет нужды в подотчётности.

### 3. Darrin Patrick — STATUS: LIMITED B / KEEP CAREFUL

**Что можно использовать только осторожно:**
- CT article on MacDonald summarizes Patrick’s 2016 firing as involving sinful issues related to pride and celebrity / identity built through ministry and media platforms.
- CT article describes his later process as extended counseling/restoration, with time away from ministry and supervised role.

**Источник:**
- Christianity Today, “Harvest Elders Say James MacDonald Is ‘Biblically Disqualified’ From Ministry,” 2019-11-05. URL: https://www.christianitytoday.com/2019/11/harvest-elders-say-james-macdonald-biblically-disqualified/

**Почему не PUBLIC core:**
- нужен archived The Journey leadership update / original elders letter;
- sensitive death history should not be dragged into article unless directly relevant and pastorally necessary;
- use only for restoration-process nuance, not as scandal illustration.

**Смысловая ценность:**
Не годится для “скандального” блока. Может пригодиться как осторожный counter-example для темы: restoration process, supervised time, leading with a limp, and not turning every fall into the same category.

### 4. Perry Noble — STATUS: HOLD

**Причина HOLD:**
- поисковый проход дал leads на Greenville News / NewSpring announcement, но прямой stable official/near-primary source в этом проходе не закрыт;
- пока не печатать как подтверждённый кейс в публичной статье;
- можно оставить как internal lead: alcohol-related removal, family neglect, later return/platform debate, but not cite until direct source is captured.

### 5. Итоговое правило после слоя U

Публичное ядро пока:
- Robert Morris — PUBLIC A;
- SBC/Guidepost — PUBLIC A-/B+;
- RZIM/Ravi Zacharias — PUBLIC with report chain;

- Mark Driscoll — LIMITED/HOLD depending on access to Acts 29/Mars Hill original docs.

Hold / do not publish yet:
- Perry Noble;
- Tullian Tchividjian;
- Darrin Patrick as scandal core;
- any claims relying on comments, blogs, deleted pages, social screenshots without archive.

### Главная новая формула

Верификация должна отвечать не на вопрос “известный ли это скандал?”, а на вопрос: **какую точную фразу мы можем напечатать так, чтобы она выдержала проверку источника?**

# v2026-06-25V — case verification tightening: concrete printable claims only

Date: 2026-06-25. Mode: STRICT CASE VERIFICATION. No forbidden encyclopedia. No comment-section evidence. No case enters PUBLIC unless the exact printable phrase is supported by official statement, court record, independent report, or strong near-primary source quoting the original body.

## Core rule added

A case is not “verified” in the abstract. Only a sentence is verified. For every proposed sentence ask:

1. Who says this?
2. Is it official, court-level, independent report, or journalism quoting official text?
3. Can we print this sentence without adding one word beyond the source?
4. Does the label match the source-level?

# v2026-06-25W — strict case verification pass: LIMITED/HOLD tightening after primary-source search

## Operating rule for this pass

This pass did **not** try to add more names for effect. It tested HOLD/LIMITED cases against a stricter publication rule:

> A case is not “verified” as a whole. Only a precise printable sentence is verified when it is tied to a stable source level: official statement, court/independent report, or responsible near-primary reporting.

No encyclopedia sources are used as evidentiary basis. Search snippets that surfaced encyclopedia summaries were treated only as leads and were not imported as sources.

## Steven Lawson — status: LIMITED B+ / not public-core yet

### What is printable with attribution

- Steven Lawson was removed/fired from ministry at Trinity Bible Church of Dallas after admitting an inappropriate relationship.
- In March 2025, after months of silence, he publicly stated that he had sinned grievously by having a sinful relationship with a woman not his wife.
- He framed his later silence as time needed to search his soul and determine that his repentance was real.

### Source status

- Near-primary / responsible reporting: Chron article with Lawson's own public apology language and reporting on removal/resignations.
- Still needed for PUBLIC A/B+ status: preserved direct Trinity Bible Church statement and direct institutional statements from OnePassion / Master's Seminary / Ligonier, if available.

### Classification

- `hidden sexual sin + delayed public apology + repentance-language case`
- Useful for the repentance chapter, not as a criminal/abuse case unless separately proven.

### Safe use

Use Lawson only for the narrow pattern:

> A respected conservative preacher may use very strong repentance language after exposure; the question for the church is not whether the words sound orthodox, but what facts are verified, what accountability exists, and whether public trust/qualification has been restored by more than a statement.

### Do not say

- Do not call it criminal.
- Do not claim abuse, coercion, student status, duration, or age gap unless tied to a strong direct source.
- Do not write “he repented” as a fact; write “he publicly said...” or “he described his conduct as...”

Source: https://www.chron.com/culture/religion/article/texas-pastor-affair-x-fired-20220162.php

# v2026-06-25X — CASE VERIFICATION STRICT PASS: HOLD CASES AND SOURCE-TIER DISCIPLINE

Scope of this pass: continue verification of the modern case atlas, but only by exact, printable, source-proportional claims. No new files were created. This layer tightens several HOLD/LIMITED statuses and prevents attractive but under-sourced examples from entering the public core.

## Non-negotiable rule added

A case is not "verified" as a whole. A single printable sentence is verified or not verified.

Use this test before any public sentence:

1. Can we name the source tier? A = court / official report / official church or ministry statement; B = reputable journalism quoting the official source; C = lead only.
2. Can we print the sentence without filling gaps from memory?
3. Does the sentence avoid upgrading the source? Example: "reported by X" is not the same as "proved by X".
4. Does the sentence avoid theological over-classification? Example: leadership misconduct is not automatically heresy; adultery is not automatically predatory abuse; platform return is not automatically full pastoral restoration.
5. Does the sentence preserve the difference between forgiveness, fellowship, office, public teaching platform, and elder qualification?

## Status changes / confirmations in this pass

### Perry Noble — KEEP HOLD / DO NOT USE IN PUBLIC CORE

Current source status: HOLD.

Reason: available leads point toward removal from NewSpring over alcohol-related personal conduct and neglect of family, and later dispute over qualification to pastor; however, in this pass no durable accessible primary NewSpring statement was captured in the pack. Do not print strong claims beyond internally noted leads until a stable primary page, archive capture, or reliable full-text article is captured.

Do not publish:
- "NewSpring said he was unqualified to pastor" unless direct wording is captured.
- "restoration was invalid" as a factual conclusion.
- "alcohol abuse" as an interpretive label unless tied to the exact source wording.

Possible use if primary is later captured: restoration-speed / qualification / founder-platform dynamics.

### Darrin Patrick — KEEP HOLD FOR PUBLIC ARTICLE; LIMITED FOR INTERNAL TYPOLOGY ONLY

Current source status: HOLD for public article, LIMITED for internal typology.

Reason: leads point to removal by The Journey elders for pastoral misconduct and historical pattern language, but this pass did not capture the original The Journey elder letter or a stable full-text near-primary page. Until that is closed, do not use as a public proof case.

Do not publish exact language such as:
- "historical pattern of sin";
- "inappropriate meetings, conversations, and phone calls";
- "domineering / misuse of power";
unless the original letter or a stable near-primary source is captured in the pack.

Possible later use: restoration-process case, not abuse-core case.

### Mark Driscoll / Mars Hill — KEEP LIMITED, NOT PUBLIC CORE

Current source status: LIMITED.

Reason: the Acts 29 language is widely cited and appears in leads, but this pass still treats it as insufficient for exact quotation unless an archived official Acts 29 statement is captured. Without that, public article may only use broad, sourced phrasing from high-quality secondary reporting, and even then only for domineering/disqualifying leadership, not heresy, not sexual scandal, not criminal conduct.

Allowed if source captured later:
- co-founder / network separation;
- leadership style and disciplinary concerns;
- recommended stepping away for a period.

Forbidden without primary capture:
- exact quotation of Acts 29 phrases;
- calling him a wolf or false teacher;
- treating the case as equivalent to criminal abuse cases.

### Tullian Tchividjian — LIMITED, NOT CORE

Current source status: LIMITED.

Publicly safe at limited level: resignation after admitted affair, if tied to reliable reporting.

Not yet closed enough for stronger claims:
- PCA deposition details;
- Coral Ridge elder process;
- second affair chronology;
- restoration legitimacy.

Use only for the narrow pattern: quick ministry re-entry / public repentance language / distinction between forgiveness and office. Do not make him a central proof case unless primary denominational/church documents are captured.

### Steve Lawson — LIMITED B+, NOT CORE

Current source status: LIMITED B+.

Use only for hidden sexual sin + delayed public apology + strong language of personal sin. Do not classify as abuse/criminal unless evidence changes. Do not overstate the source. This case is useful as a modern example of public orthodox preaching and hidden sin, but it is not currently a system-abuse case in the pack.

### Art Azurdia — LIMITED B, KEEP NARROW

Current source status: LIMITED B.

Allowed use: own confession of adultery, self-disqualification, hidden sin while exercising ministry, and the important pastoral observation that God may genuinely bless hearers through a compromised preacher without thereby justifying the preacher or preserving his qualification.

Forbidden:
- treating survivor testimony as court/institutional finding;
- asserting exact conference-platform claims without primary/archived conference source;
- calling the case fully closed as abuse case.

### James MacDonald — KEEP PUBLIC B+

Current source status: PUBLIC B+.

Use as non-sexual disqualification case: harmful conduct, spiritual/positional authority misuse, governance failure, bullying/intimidation, lack of evident fruits of repentance, if tied to the reporting that quotes Harvest elder statements. This is important because the series must show that disqualification is not only about adultery or criminal abuse.

### Josh Buice — KEEP LIMITED B

Current source status: LIMITED B.

Use as hidden slander / anonymous account / delayed confession after evidence. Not an abuse case. Not criminal. Do not inflate.

## Public-core recommendation after this pass

The public article should currently rely on:

1. Robert Morris — criminal child sexual abuse; euphemism prohibition.
2. SBC / Guidepost — institutional failure, information control, survivor resistance.
3. RZIM / Ravi Zacharias — independent investigation, platform predator pattern, posthumous collapse of trusted apologetics brand.
4. Willow Creek / Bill Hybels — credible allegations in independent review; board failure; leadership culture.
5. James MacDonald — non-sexual disqualification: authority misuse, bullying, governance, lack of fruits.

Use only in sidebars / internal typology unless further closed:
- Azurdia;
- Buice;
- Lawson;
- Driscoll;
- Tullian.

Keep HOLD:
- Perry Noble;
- Darrin Patrick.

## Core theological principle extracted

A powerful case is not the case with the most dramatic story, but the case where the article can say less and prove more.

The series should teach readers to distinguish:

- sin confessed vs sin exposed;
- apology vs repentance;
- forgiveness vs office;
- ministry fruit in hearers vs qualification of the minister;
- public usefulness vs biblical fitness;
- source lead vs printable proof.

## Wording guardrail

Write:
"In the sources currently captured, this case can only be used for..."

Do not write:
"This proves..." unless the source tier is A or B+ and the claim is directly supported.
